app. HDR maker lets you stack a series of photos with different exposure settings to create a true HDR image. The app also comes with several tone mapping algorithms that converts HDR image back to SDR image. \r\n\r\nIf you are wondering how the magic happens behind the screen, here is a good explanation: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=bkQJdaGGVM8\r\n\r\nYou can use this app to develop raw files.
